    <script language="javascript">
     function _CF_checkEmail(object_value, required)
		{
		// trim whitespace before we validate
		object_value = object_value.replace(/^\s+/,'').replace(/\s+$/,'');
		
		email_pattern = /^\w+([-+.']\w+)*@\w+([-.]\w+)*\.\w+([-.]\w+)*$/;
		
		return email_pattern.test(object_value);
		}
		function check()
		{
			if(document.getElementById("inputEmail").value=="")
			{
				document.getElementById("message").innerHTML="&lt;font color='red'&gt;Please fill your login name to retrieve the login password.&lt;/font&gt;";
				return false;
			}
			else if(!_CF_checkEmail(document.getElementById("inputEmail").value,true))
			{
				document.getElementById("message").innerHTML="&lt;font color='red'&gt; Please fill in valid email address!&lt;/font&gt;";
				return false;
			}else{
				var inputEmail=document.getElementById("inputEmail").value;
				var params="LoginName="+inputEmail;
				$.ajax({type:"get",
					   url:jsMainSiteUrl+"ActionCom/CheckUserNameAjax.cfm",
					   data:params,
					   async:false,
					   success:function(result){
						   result=$.trim(result);
						   if(result=="true"){
								document.getElementById("message").innerHTML="&lt;font color='red'&gt;Email not found.&lt;/font&gt;";
						   }else{
							   document.getElementById("message").innerHTML="";
							}
						},
						error:function(result){
							
						}
				});
			}
			if(document.getElementById("message").innerHTML==""){
				return true;
			}else{
				return false;
			}
		}
    </script>
